Accessibility digest

Synopsis
PageHorizon House contact form
URLhttps://horizonhouse.org/contact-us/
Requesterpool@jpdev.pro

Score884
Tested byTestaro, procedure ts24
Scored byTestilo, procedure tsp24
Digested byTestilo, procedure tdp24

Introduction

This is a digest of results from a battery of accessibility Tests.

The battery includes 1353 automated accessibility tests drawn from ten different packages: Alfa, Axe, Continuum, Equal Access, HTML CodeSniffer, Nu Html Checker, QualWeb, Tenon, Testaro, and WAVE.

These tests were run on the web page named above and gave the page a score of 884, where 0 would be perfect.

Issue summary

Special issues

log: Score 74. This is based on the amount of browser error logging and miscellaneous logging during the tests.

Classified issues

Issue contentBeyondLandmarks

WCAG: 1.3.6

Score: 152

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r57, score 126 (Perceivable text content is not included in any landmark)
  • Package axe, test region, score 24 (Some page content is not contained by landmarks)
  • Package ibm, test Rpt_Aria_OrphanedContent_Native_Host_Sematics, score 36 (Content does not reside within an element with a landmark role)

Issue focusIndication

WCAG: 2.4.7

Score: 62

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test focInd, score 17 (Focused element displays no or a nostandard focus indicator)
  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R62, score 53 (Element in the sequential focus order has no visible focus)

Issue focusableOperable

WCAG: 2.1.1

Score: 53

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test focOp, score 51 (Operable elements that cannot be Tab-focused and vice versa)

Issue textContrastAA

WCAG: 1.4.3

Score: 44

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r69, score 20 (Text outside widget has subminimum contrast)
  • Package axe, test color-contrast, score 22 (Element has insufficient color contrast)
  • Package ibm, test IBMA_Color_Contrast_WCAG2AA, score 12 (Contrast ratio of text with background does not meet WCAG 2.1 AA)
  • Package wave, test c:contrast, score 18 (Very low contrast)

Issue linkIndication

WCAG: 1.3.3

Score: 38

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test linkUl, score 36 (Non-underlined adjacent links)

Issue controlNoText

WCAG: 4.1.2

Score: 36

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.1_3_1.F68, score 24 (Form control has no label)
  • Package wave, test e:label_missing, score 24 (form element has no label)

Issue errorReferenceBad

WCAG: 3.3.1

Score: 27

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R41, score 25 (Error message describes no invalid form field value)

Issue roleBad

WCAG: 4.1.2

Score: 23

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test role, score 21 (Nonexistent or implicit-overriding role)
  • Package ibm, test Rpt_Aria_ContentinfoWithNoMain_Implicit, score 1 (Element has a contentinfo role when no element has a main role)

Issue contrastAAA

WCAG: 1.4.6

Score: 21

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r66, score 16 (Text contrast less than AAA requires)
  • Package axe, test color-contrast-enhanced, score 5 (Element has insufficient color contrast (Level AAA))
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.1_4_6.G17.Fail, score 3 (Text has insufficient contrast)

Issue labelBadID

WCAG: 1.3.1

Score: 21

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package htmlcs, test w:AAA.1_3_1.H44.NonExistentFragment, score 4 (Label for attribute references a nonexistent element)
  • Package ibm, test WCAG20_Label_RefValid, score 16 (for attribute does not reference a non-empty, unique id attribute of an input element)
  • Package wave, test a:label_orphaned, score 4 (Orphaned form label)

Issue duplicateID

WCAG: 4.1.1

Score: 20

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r3, score 8 (Element id attribute value is not unique)
  • Package axe, test duplicate-id-aria, score 4 (id attribute used in ARIA or in a label has a value that is not unique)
  • Package continuum, test 94, score 8 (Element contains an id attribute set to a value that is not unique in the DOM)
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.4_1_1.F77, score 4 (Duplicate id attribute value)
  • Package ibm, test RPT_Elem_UniqueId, score 8 (Element id attribute value is not unique within the document)
